 shrikrishna ke mohak rup kaa varnak kai dharmik granthon main kiya gaya he
 a crown on the head, peacock feathers in the crown, a garland of peetambara, flute and veyjayanti
 aise adbhoot rup ko jo ekbar dekh letaa tha, wo usee kaa das banakar rah jaataa tha
 We all know that Shri Krishna loved milk, curd and butter, but apart from that he also loved a lot
 shrikrishna ko in paanch chizon se vishesh lagaav tha
 Today, on the occasion of Janmashtami, any devotee who puts these five things in front of God and prays for him sincerely, bal-gopal Kanhaiya fulfills his wish
 1
 The flute is very much loved by Shri Krishna
 ek chand main to radha ne shrikrishna kii bansuri ke bhagya ko apane bhagya se kahin shreshth bataaya he kyonki wo unke adharon ko chooti he
 After listening to the sweet melody of Shri Krishna's flute, all the gopis, gwal-bal, cows, fauna, trees and creeks used to stop
 bansuri saralata or mithaas kaa pratik he
 While decorating the idol of Shri Krishna on the occasion of Janmashtami, do not forget to keep the flute
 2
 Morpankha Bhagwan Shri Krishna wears a peacock in his crown
 mor pankh sammohan or bhavyata kaa pratik he
 It is a sign of happiness in life by removing sorrows
 kanha ke mukut kii sajaavat mor pankh ke bina adhuri he
 3
 mishri kii mithaskrishna ko maakhan mishri bahut hi priy he
 Mishri is a symbol of sweetness
 jivan main mithaas kaa hona behad jaruri he
 Shri Krishna always taught to love
 prem har us cheez se jo hamaare ird-gird maujuud he
 4
 vaijayanti kii malabhagwan shrikrishna apane gale main sadaiv vaijayanti kii maala dhaaran kiye rahete hai
 Don't forget Shri Krishna's veneration of Vyjayanti during the time of worship
 5
 Pitamber and Sandalwood's Tilakashikrishna always wore Pitamber
 maathe par chandan kaa tilak
 Devote sandalwood to them before worshiping the Lord

 "though PTI had withdrawn its complaint, PEMRA decided to impose the penalty even after such misinformation was against the spirit of the TV channel license issued to the channel owners by the regulator," the official said
 
 " PEMRA also said that the decision to impose fines on TV channels is aimed at upholding the standards of journalism
